< Text>
I attended a screening of the documentary, Be Natural, directed by Pamela Green here. This was my first time at the Harmony Preview House and I was pretty impressed. The theater had ample seating and great quality sound and picture. My only gripe, as noted in another review, are the chairs. I am 5'4" and I found myself adjusting my seat every few minutes or so because I couldn't get comfortable. The seats are on the older side and made from cloth. The only perk was that the aisles were pretty wide so people were able to pass by with ease. Overall, it's a cute little venue for private events and I'd come back if invited.< /Text>
